+     message(sprintf("- plan('%s') ...", strategy))

+     ## Explicit future
+     x <- list()
+     f <- future({
+       x$a <- 1
+       x
+     })
+     rm(list = "x")
+     y <- value(f)
+     print(y)
+     stopifnot(identical(y, y0))
+ 
+     ## Explicit future (lazy)
+     x <- list()
+     f <- future({
+       x$a <- 1
+       x

+     rm(list = "x")

+     print(y)
+     stopifnot(identical(y, y0))
